dattāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ yatra apaḥ tanayaiḥ śraddhayā anvitaiḥ yāvantaḥ ca tilāḥ pitṛ karmaṇi tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi pitaraḥ svarga vāsinaḥ pitṛ lokeṣu ye kecid sarveṣām pitaraḥ sthitāḥ tarpyamāṇāḥ parām tṛptim yānti gaṅgā jalaiḥ śubhaiḥ yaḥ icchet saphalam janma saṃtatim vā śubha ānane sa pitṝn tarpayet gaṅgām abhigamya surān tathā ye kecid pitaraḥ puṇya śīlinaḥ māsam tarpaṇa mātreṇa piṇḍa saṃpātanena ca gaṅgāyām pitaraḥ sarve su prītāḥ sūrya varcasaḥ apsaraḥ gaṇaṇa saṃyuktān hema ratna vibhūṣitān muktā jāla paricchannān veṇu vīṇā nināditān bherī śaṅkha mṛdaṅga ādi nirghoṣān sraj vibhūṣitān brahya lokam prayānti hi gaṅgāyām tu naraḥ snātvā yaḥ nityam liṅgam arcayet agnihotrāṇi vedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca bahu dakṣiṇāḥ gaṅgāyām liṅga pūjāyāḥ koṭi aṃśena api no samāḥ pitṝn udiśya vā devān gaṅgā ambhibhiḥ prasiṃcayet tṛptāḥ syuḥ tasya pitaraḥ naraka sthāḥ ca tad kṣaṇāt mṛd kumbhāt tāmra kumbhaiḥ tu snānam daśaguṇam smṛtam raupyaiḥ śataguṇam puṇyam hemaiḥ koṭi guṇam smṛtam tara viśeṣeṇa phalam ca eva uttarottaram devānām darśanam puṇyam darśanāt sparśanam varam sparśanāt arcanam śreṣṭham ghṛta snānam atas param prāhuḥ gaṅgā jalaiḥ snānam ghṛta snāna samam budhāḥ arghyam dravya viśeṣeṇa gaṅgā toyena yaḥ sakṛt apaḥ kṣīram kuśa agrāṇi ghṛtam dadhi tathā madhu aṣṭāṅgaiḥ eṣa yuktaḥ uraghaḥ bhānave parikīrtitaḥ viṣṇoḥ śivasya sūryasya durgāyāḥ brahmaṇaḥ tathā gaṅgā tīre pratiṣṭhām tu yaḥ karoti nara uttamaḥ tathā eva āyatanāni eṣām kārayati api śaktitas anya tīrtheṣu karaṇāt koṭi guṇam bhavet gaṅgā tīra samudbhūta mṛdā ligāni śaktitas sa lakṣaṇāni kṛtvā tu pratiṣṭhāpya dine dine mantriḥ ca patra puṣpa ādyaiḥ pūjayitvā ca śaktitas sarva ānanda pradāyinyām gaṅgāyām yaḥ nara uttamaḥ namaḥ nārāyaṇāya iti praṇava ādyam niyamya ca bhavataḥ sarvāḥ hi upatiṣṭhanti siddhayaḥ namaḥ śivāya iti mantram sa tāram vidhinā tu yaḥ caturviśati lakṣam vai japet sākṣāt sa śaṃkaraḥ pañcākṣarī siddhavidyā śivaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ pūjitāyām tu gaṅgāyām pūjitāḥ sarva devatāḥ catur bhujām tri netrām ca sarva avayava śobhitām ratna kumbha sita ambhoja vara abhaya karam śubhām śveta vastra parīdhānām muktāmaṇi vibhūṣitām su prasannām su vadanām karuṇā ārdra hṛd ambujām sudhā plāvita bhū pṛṣṭhām trailokya namitām sadā dhyātvā jala mayīm gaṅgām pūjayan puṇya bhāj bhavet vaiśākha śukla saptamyām jahnunā jāhnavī purā krodhāt pītā punar tyaktā karṇa raṅghrāt tu dakṣiṇāt tām tatra pūjayet devīm gaṅgām gagana mekhalām akṣayāyām tu vaiśākhe kārttike api śubha ānane rātrau jāgaraṇam kṛtvā yava annaiḥ ca tilaiḥ tathā viṣṇum gaṅgām ca śaṃbhum ca pūjayet bhakti bhāvatas kalpa koṭi sahasrāṇi kalpa koṭi śatāni ca divyam vimānam āsthāya viṣṇu loke mahīyate tatas mahī talam prāpya rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ bhuktvā vividha saukhyāni rūpa śīla guṇa anvitaḥ dehānte jñānavān bhūtvā śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt yajñaḥ dānam tapaḥ japyam śrāddham ca sura pūjanam gaṅgāyām tu kṛtam sarvam koṭi koṭi guṇam bhavet yaḥ tu akṣayatṛtīyāyām gaṅgā tīre dadāti vai ghṛtadhenum vidhānena tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu kalpa koṭi sahasrāṇi kalpa koṭi śatāni ca sahasra āditya saṃkāśaḥ sarva kāma samanvitaḥ tatas tu jāyate vipraḥ gaṅgā tīre dhana anvitaḥ ante tu brahma vid bhūtvā mokṣam āpnoti asaṃśayaḥ ratna kāñcana bhū pūrṇe śīla vidyā yaśas nvite mokṣa bhāgī na atra kāryā vicāraṇā bhūmim nivartana mitām gaṅgā tīre dadāti yaḥ bhūmi reṇu pramāṇa abdam brahma viṣṇu śiva atigaḥ bherī śaṅkha ādi nirghoṣaiḥ gīta vāditra niḥsvanaiḥ naraka sthān pitṝn sarvān prāpayitvā divam tathā svarga sthitān mokṣayitvā svayam jñānī ca mohini ante jñāna asinā chitvā avidyām pañca parvikām sapta hastena daṇḍena triṃśat daṇḍāḥ nivartanam tri bhāga hīnam gocarma mānam āha vidhiḥ svayam grāmam gaṅgā taṭe yaḥ vai brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati brahma viṣṇu śiva prītye durgāyāḥ bhāskarasya ca sahasra guṇitam tat tu vijñeyam grāma dāyinaḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśe vimāne vaiṣṇave pure krīḍate śāṅkare vā api stutaḥ deva ādibhiḥ mudā bhūmi reṇu abda saṃkhyākam kālam sthitvā ca tatra saḥ aṇima ādi guṇaiḥ yukte yoginām jāyate kule akṣayāyām tu yaḥ devi svarṇam ṣoḍaśa māsikam anna dānāt viṣṇu lokam śaivam vai tila dānāt gāndharvam svarṇa vāsobhiḥ kīrtim kanyā pradānāt vidyayā mukti dam jñānam prāpya yāyāt nirañjanam naraḥ yaḥ tu nānā vṛkṣaiḥ samanvitam mahā ārāmam kārayet bhaktyā gṛham ca upavana anvitam kadala nārikeraiḥ ca kapittha aśoka campakaiḥ panasaiḥ bilva vṛkṣaiḥ ca kadamba aśvattha pāṭalaiḥ bhāgaiḥ tālaiḥ nāgaraṅgaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ anyaiḥ ca saṃyutam mātī vijaya saṃyuktam tathā pāṭala rājitam nicitam kārayitvā evam āvāsam puṣpa śobhitam śivāya viṣṇave vā api durgāyai bhāskarāya ca tasya puṇya phalam vakṣye saṃkṣepāt na tu vistarāt yāvanti teṣām vṛkṣāṇām puṣpa mūla phalāni ca bījāni ca vicitrāṇi teṣām mūlāni vai tathā tāvat kalpa sahasrāṇi teṣām lokeṣu saṃsthitiḥ iti śrī bṛhat nāradīya purāṇa uttara bhāge mohinīvasu saṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye dānādividhivarṇanam nāma ekacatvāriṃśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ dhanyā aham kṛtakṛtyā aham sa phalam jīvitam mama yat śrutam tvad mukha ambhojāt gā māhātmyam uttamam aho gaṅgā samam tīrtham na asti kiṃcid dharā tale yasyāḥ saṃdarśana ādīnām īdṛśam puṇyam īritam guḍadhenu ādi dhenūnām vidhānam ca yathākramam uvāca tat śrutvā mohinī vākyam vasuḥ tasyāḥ purohitaḥ veda āgamānām tattva jñaḥ smayamānaḥ uvāca ha śṛṇu mohini vakṣyāmi yat pṛṣṭam hi tvayā mama guḍadhenu vidhānam ca yathā śāstre prakīrtitam kṛṣṇājinam catur grīvam vinyaset bhuvi gomayena upaliptāyām kuśān āstīrya yatnatas prac mukhīm kalpayet dhenum udak pādām sa vatsakām uttamā guḍadhenuḥ tu catur bhāraiḥ prakīrtitā vatsam bhāreṇa kurvīta bhārābhyām madhyamā smṛtā ardha bhāreṇa vatsaḥ syāt kaniṣṭhā bhārakeṇa tu caturtha aṃśena vatsaḥ syāt gṛha vitta anusārataḥ dhenu vatsau ghṛtasya etau sita ślakṣṇa ambara āvṛtau śukti karṇau ikṣu pādau śuddha muktā āla īkṣaṇau tāmra gaṇḍūka pṛṣṭhau tau sita cāmara lomakau kāṃsya dohau indranīla maṇi kalpita tārakau suvarṇa śṛṅga ābharaṇau śuddha raupya khurau ubhau nānā phalam samāyuktau ghrāṇa gandha karaṇḍakau yā lakṣmīḥ sarva bhūtānām yā ca deveṣu avasthitā dhenu rūpeṇa sā devī mama śāntim prayacchatu deha sthā yā ca rudrāṇām śaṃkarasya sadā priyā dhenu rūpeṇa sā devī mama pāpam vyapohatu viṣṇoḥ vakṣasi yā lakṣmīḥ svāhā rūpā vibhāvasoḥ candra arka śakra śaktiḥ yā dhenu rūpā astu sā śriye lakṣmīḥ yā lokapālānām sā dhenuḥ vara dā astu mama svadhā yā pitṛ mukhyānām svāhā yajña mujā ca yā sarva pāpa harā dhenuḥ sā me śāntim prayacchatu tām dhenum brāhmaṇāya nivedayet paṭhyate yāḥ tu pāpar vināśinyaḥ kīrtitāḥ daśa dhenavaḥ tāsām svarūpam vakṣyāmi śāstra ukam śṛṇu mohini prathamā guḍadhenuḥ syāt ghṛtadhenuḥ atha aparā tiladhenuḥ tṛtīyā ca caturthā jala saṃjñitā pañcamī kṣīradhenuḥ ca ṣaṣṭhī madhu mayī smṛtā saptamā śarkarādhenuḥ dadhidhenuḥ tathā aṣṭamā ratnadhenuḥ ca navamī daśamī tu svarūpāt kumbhāḥ syuḥ drava dhenūnām ca itarāsām tu rāśayaḥ mantra āvāhana saṃyuktāḥ sadā parvaṇi parvaṇi yathāśraddham pradātavyāḥ bhukti mukti phala pradāḥ aneka yajña phala dāḥ sarva pāpa harāḥ śubhāḥ ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte athavā punar tīrtheṣu sva gṛhe vā api gaṅgā tīre viśeṣataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vipram dakṣiṇābhiḥ pratoṣya ca tatas saṃpūjayet gaṅgām vidhinā su samāhitaḥ aṣṭa mūrti dharām devīm divya rūpām nirīkṣya ca pāyasam kārayitvā ca da tvā madhu ghṛtam tathā tad pāyasam apūpān ca modakāḥ maṇḍalāni ca tathā guñjā ardha mātram ca suvarṇam rūpyam eva ca bilva pattrāṇi dūrvāḥ ca rocanā sita candanam nīlotpalāni ca anyāni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca yathāśakti mahā bhaktyā gaṅgāyām ca eva nikṣipet om gaṅgāyai nārāyaṇyai śivāyai ca namaḥ namaḥ paurṇamāsyām apāyām vā kāryam prātar samāhitaiḥ haviṣya āśī mita āhāraḥ brahmacarya samanvitaḥ saṃvatsara ante tasya iṣā gaṅgā divya vapurdharā divya mālya aṃbarā ca eva divya ratna vibhūṣitā pratyakṣa rūpā puratas tiṣṭati eva vara pradā evam pratyakṣa rūpām tām gaṅgām divya vapurdharām dṛṣṭvā sva cakṣuṣā martyaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ bhavet śubhe yān yān kāmayate martyaḥ kāmān tān tān avāpnuyāt ca mayā uditam te pṛṣṭam hi sarvam guḍadhenu pūrvam gaṅgā arcanam mukti karam vratam sāṃvatsaram śrīpati tuṣṭi dam hi iti śrī bṛhat nāradīya purāṇa uttara bhāge mohinīvasu saṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye guḍadhenuvidhikathanam nāma dvicatvāriṃśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca vasoḥ vacanam ākarṇya gaṅgā māhātmya sūcakam śrutam vipra mayā sarvam go dāna ādi śubha āvaham gaṅgā ādīnām pūjanam ca sthāpanam tatra vā dvija kim phalam vada sarvajña tvām aham śaraṇam gatā adhunā gati dātā tvam varjitāyāḥ ca bandhubhiḥ patyā virahitā ca aham putra hīnā vidām vara tvām eva śaraṇam prāptā pituḥ vacana gauravāt tat bhavān praṇatāyāḥ me gaṅgāmāhātmyam saṃyutam uvāca tat śrutvā mohinī vākyam vasuḥ vipraḥ pratāpavān sabhājya mohinīm bhūpa prāha veda vidām varaḥ sādhu pṛṣṭam tvayā devi lokānām hita kāmyayā gaṅgā māhātmyam akhilam mahā pāpa praṇāśanam vṛṣadhvajena kathitam śivena dayayā purā prītyā devyā abhi pṛṣṭena gaṅgā tīra nivāsinā devaiḥ tu bhuktam pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne ṛṣibhiḥ tathā aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ śarvarṃyām guhyaka ādibhaiḥ upavāsāt vāram bhaikṣyam bhaikṣyāt varam a yācitam a yācita dvāram naktam tasmāt naktam samācaret haviṣya bhojanam snānam satyam āhāra lāghavam agnikāryam adhaḥśayyām nakta āśī ṣaṣ samācaret gaṅgā tīre māgha māse yaḥ kuryāt naktabhojanam śivāyatana pārśve tu kṛsaram ghṛta saṃyutam naivedyam ca nivedya eva kṛsara annam śivasya tu kāṣṭha maunena bhuñjānaḥ jihvā laulyam vivarjayet palāśa patre bhuñjānaḥ śivam smṛtvā jita indriyaḥ dharmarājasya devyāḥ ca pṛthak piṇḍam prakalpayet sa upavāsaḥ caturddaśyām bhavet ubhaya pakṣayoḥ paurṇamāsyām tu gandhaiḥ ca gaṅgāyāḥ salilaiḥ tathā śivam saṃsnāpya payasā madhu ājya dadhibhiḥ pṛthak tatas dadyāt tu śaktyā eva apūpam ca ghṛta pācitam tila āḍhakam pragṛhya atha śiva liṅga upari kṣipet nīlotpalaiḥ ca sarva īśam pūjayet paṅkajaiḥ api dadyāt bhaktyā maheśāya tathā pattra phalāni ca kṛṣṇa go mithunam ca eva sarūpam ca nivedayet bhojayet brāhmaṇān aṣṭau māsa ante tu sa dakṣiṇān madhu māṃsam ca tam māsam brahmacaryavān evam kṛtvā yathoddiṣṭam eka vāram idam vratam yamaiḥ ca niyamaiḥ yuktaḥ śraddhā bhakti parāyaṇaḥ indranīla pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ śikhi saṃyuktaiḥ gatvā śiva puram ramyam sarva sva kula saṃyutaḥ bhuktvā bhogān aśeṣān ca yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam tatas bhavati dharma ātmā jambūdvīpa patiḥ tathā tatra bhuṅkte samastān ca bhogān vigata kalmaṣaḥ surūpaḥ subhagaḥ ca eva tathā vihita śāsanaḥ vaiśākhe śuklapakṣe vā caturdaśyām samāhitaḥ śālyannam kṣīra saṃyuktam yaḥ kuryāt naktabhojanam śivam saṃpūjya puṣpa ādyaiḥ bhojyam tu saṃnivedya ca kāṣṭha maunena bhuñjānaḥ vaṭa kāṣṭena vai tathā śiva liṅga samīpe tu gaṅgā tīre niśi svapet paurṇamāsyām prabhāte tu gaṅgāyām vidhinā tathā snātvā upavāsam saṃkalpya kuryāt jāgaraṇam niśi liṅgam ghṛtena saṃsnāpya puṣpa gandha ādibhiḥ tathā naivedya dhūpa dīpaiḥ ca saṃpūjya vṛṣabham śubham brāhmaṇān ca yathāśakti pāyasena tu bhojayet tapaḥ kṛtvā tu niyamāt yat puṇyam tat asaṃśayam su śveta vṛṣa yuktaiḥ ca muktā jāla vibhūṣitaiḥ svakīya pitṛbhiḥ sārdham prayāti īśvara mandiram nīlotpala suṃgandhābhiḥ surūpābhiḥ samantataḥ kāntābhiḥ divya rūpābhiḥ bhuktvā bhogān anekaśas jāyate sa mahīpālaḥ kīrti aiśvarya samanvitaḥ eka chattreṇa sa mahīm pālayati ājñayā saha ante vairāgya saṃpannaḥ gaṅgām sa labhate punar sa tayā śraddhayā yuktaḥ gaṅgāyām maraṇam labhet jyeṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe daśamyām hasta saṃyute gaṅgā tīre tu puruṣaḥ nārī vā bhakti bhāvataḥ niśāyām jāgaram kṛtvā gaṅgām daśavidhaiḥ tatas puṣpaiḥ gandhaiḥ ca naivedyaiḥ phalaiḥ ca daśa saṃkhyāyā tathā eva dīpaiḥ tāmbūlaiḥ pūjayet śraddhayā anvitaḥ snātvā bhaktyā tu jāhnavyām daśa kṛtvas vidhānāt daśa prasṛti kṛṣṇan ca tilān sarpiḥ ca vai jale saktu piṇḍān guḍa piṇḍān dadyāt ca daśa saṃkhyayā tatas gaṅgā taṭe ramye hemnā rūpyeṇa vā tathā gaṅgāyāḥ pratimām kṛtvā vakṣyamāṇa svarūpiṇīm saṃsthāpya pūjayet devīm tad alābhe mṛd ādi vā cāmaraiḥ vījyamānām ca śveta chatra upaśibhitām su prasannām ca vara dām karuṇā ārdra nija antarām sudhā plāvita bhū pṛṣṭhām deva ādibhiḥ abhiṣṭutām divya ratna parītām ca diṃvya mālya anulepanām dhyātvā jale yathā proktām tatra arcāyām tu pūjayet vakṣyamāṇena mantreṇa kuryāt pūjām viśeṣataḥ pañcāmṛtena ca snānam arcāyām tu viśiṣyate nārāyaṇam maheśam ca brahmānam bhāskaram tathā bhagīratham ca nṛpatim himavantam naga īśvaram daśa prasthān yavān dadyāt daśa gavyaiḥ yathāhitān kāritān vai yathāśakti svarṇena rajatena vā tad alābhe piṣṭa mayān abhyarcya kusuma ādibhiḥ gaṅgāyām prakṣipet pūrvam mantreṇa eva tu mantra vid ratha ārūḍha pratikṛtim gaṅgāyāḥ tu uttarā mukhām bhramantyāḥ darśanam loke durlabham pāpa karmaṇām durgāyāḥ ratha yātrā asti tathā eva atra api kārayet evam kṛtvā vidhānena vitta śāṭhya vivarjitaḥ daśa pāpaiḥ vakṣyamāṇaiḥ sadyas eva vimucyate adattānām upādānam hiṃsā ca eva avidhānataḥ paradāra upasevā ca kāyikam tribidham smṛtam pāṃruṣyam anṛtam vā api paiśunyam ca api sarvaśas vitatha abhiniveśaḥ ca mānasam trividham smṛtam daśa triṃśat ca tān pūrvān pitṝn eva tathā aparān uddharati eva saṃsārāt mantreṇa anena pūjitā om namaḥ daśa harāyai nārāyaṇyai gaṅgāyai namaḥ uddaret daśa pūrvāṇi parāṇi ca bhava arṇavāt vakṣyamāṇam idam stotram vidhinā pratigṛhya ca gaṅgā agre tad dine japyam viṣṇu pūjām pravartayet om namaḥ śivāyai gaṅgāyai śiva dāyai namaḥ astu te namaḥ astu viṣṇu rūpinyai gaṅgāyai te namaḥ namaḥ sarvasya sarva vyādhīnām bhiṣaj śreṣṭhe namaḥ astu te sthāṇu jaṅgama saṃbhūta viṣa hantri namaḥ astu te saṃsāra viṣa nāśinyai jīvanāyai namaḥ namaḥ śāntaye saṃtāpa hārinyai namaḥ te sarvamūrtaye sarva saṃśuddhi kārinyai namaḥ pāpa vimuktaye mandāyai liṅga dhāriṇyai nārāyaṇyai namaḥ namaḥ pṛthvyai śiva amṛtāyai ca virajāyai namaḥ namaḥ śāntāyai te pratiṣṭhāyai vara dāyai namaḥ namaḥ sarva āpad pratipakṣāyai maṅgalāyai namaḥ namaḥ gaṅgā mama agratas bhūyāt gaṅgā mama pārśvayoḥ tathā ādau tvam ante madhye ca sarvā tvam śive tvam eva mūlaprakṛtiḥ tvam hi nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ gaṅge tvam paramātmā ca śivaḥ tubhyam namaḥ namaḥ śṛṇoti śraddhayā vā api kāya vācika saṃbhavaiḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti pretya brahmaṇi līyate tasyām daśamyām etat ca stotram gaṅgā jale sthitaḥ japan tu daśa kṛtvas ca daridraḥ vā api ca akṣamaḥ saḥ api tad phalam āpnoti gaṅgām saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ yathā gaurī tathā gaṅgā tasmāt gauryāḥ tu pūjane yathā śivaḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ yathā viṣṇuḥ tathā hi umā umā yathā tathā gaṅgā ca atra bhedaḥ na vidyate viṣṇu rudra antaram yaḥ ca gagāgaurī antaram tathā lakṣmī gauryataram yaḥ ca prabrūte mūḍha dhīḥ tu saḥ śuklapakṣe divā bhūmau gaṅgāyām uttarāyaṇe ye muñcanti nara prāṇān gaṅgāyām te viṣṇu lokam gacchanti stūyamānāḥ divisthitaiḥ yā gatiḥ yoga yuktasya sātvikasya manīṣiṇaḥ sā getiḥ tyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyām tu śarīriṇaḥ anaśanam gṛhītvā yaḥ gaṅgā tīre mṛtaḥ naraḥ gaṅgāyām maraṇāt prāṇān yoḥ prājñaḥ tyaktum icchati mahān ca api gataḥ kālaḥ yatra tatra api gacchataḥ gaṅgāyām maraṇena iha na atra kāryā vicāraṇā jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ vā api kāmataḥ api vā gaṅgāyām tu mṛtaḥ martyaḥ svargam mokṣam ca vindati prāṇeṣu utsṛjyamāneṣu yaḥ gaṅgām saṃsmaret naraḥ spṛśet vā pāpa śīlaḥ api sa vai yāti parām gatim gaṅgām gatvā yaiḥ śarīram visṛṣṭam prāptāḥ dhīrāḥ te tu devaiḥ sama tvam tasmāt survān prohya mukti pradān vai sevet gaṅgām ā śarīrasya pātam antarikṣe kṣitau toye pāpīyān api yaḥ mṛtaḥ brahma viṣṇu śivaiḥ pūjyam padam akṣayyam aśnute yaḥ sa prāṇaḥ prayataḥ śiṣṭa saṃmataḥ cintayet manasā gaṅgām saḥ gatim paramām labhet bhaktyā gaṅgām smaran yāti śaivam vā vaiṣṇavam puram śaṃbhoḥ jaṭā kalāpāt tu viniṣkrāntā ati karkaśāt plāvayitvā divam ninye yā pāpān yagara ātmajān yāvanti asthīni gaṅgāyām tiṣṭhanti puruṣasya vai gaṅgā toye tu yasya asthi prāpyate śubha karmaṇaḥ gaṅgāyām maraṇe yādṛś tādṛś phalam avāpnuyāt tad asthi piṇḍam puṭake nidhāya paśyan diśam preta gaṇa upagūḍhām snātvā tatas tīrtha vaṭā kṣayam ca dṛṣṭvā pradadyāt atha dakṣiṇām tu pravāham avadhim kṛtvā yāvat hasta catuṣṭayam tatra nārāyaṇaḥ svāmī na anyaḥ svāmī kadācana na tatra pratigṛhṇīyāt prāṇaiḥ kaṇṭha gataiḥ api bhādra śukla caturdaśyām yāvat ākramate jalam tāvat gabham vijānīyāt tat dūram tīram ucyate sārdha hasta śatam yāvat garbhaḥ tīram tatas param iti kānām matam devi śruti smṛtiṣu saṃmatam tīrāt gavyūti mātram tu paritas kṣetram ucyate tīram tyaktvā vaset kṣetre tīre vāsaḥ na ca iṣyate eka yojana vistīrṇā kṣetra sīmā taṭa dvayāt gaṅgā sīmām na laghanti pāpāni api akhilāni api tām tu dṛṣṭvā palāyante yathā siṃham vanaukasaḥ yatra gaṅgā mahābhāge rāma śaṃbhu tapaḥ vanam tīrthe na pratigṛhṇīyāt puṇyeṣu āyataneṣu ca tīrthe yaḥ pratigṛhṇāti puṇyeṣu āyataneṣu ca gaṅgā vikrayāṇāt devi viṣṇoḥ vikrayaṇam bhavet gaṅgā tīra samudbhūtām ma dam mūrghnā bibharti yaḥ gaṅgā pulina jām dhūlim āstīrya atha nijān pitṝn prīṇayan yaḥ naraḥ piṇḍān dadyāt tān svar nayet api paṭhan śṛṇvan naraḥ hi eti tat viṣṇoḥ paramam padam vaiṣṇavīm gatim icchadbhiḥ śaivīm vā vidhinandini iti śrī bṛhat nāradīya purāṇa uttara bhāge mohinīvasu saṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye pūjādikatham nāma tricatvāriṃśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ
